              <noteGrp>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">
                  <p>6.38.3 to 6.38.8 are in different metre (perhaps Indravajrā) with the
                    same content.</p>
                  <p>6.38.8 has only first hemistich.</p>
                  <p>Missing verses 6.38.30ab.</p>
                  <p>Metre break 6.38.13ab 6.38.17ab 6.38.21cd 6.38.28ab.</p>
                </note>

                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.39: <p>Missing verses 109ab, 110cd,
                    114cd, 115ab, 116cd, 117, 118, 119ab , 121cd, 122, 123ab, 125cd, 130,
                    131, 132, 133, 134ab, 135cd, 136, 137ab, 144ab, 147cd, 148ab, 137cd,
                    167, 171cd, 172, 173, 174, 190, 191, 193cd, 195, 196, 197, 198ab,
                    200cd, 201ab, 202ab, 204cd, 205, 206, 207, 211cd, 216ab, 219, 220,
                    221, 222, 223, 224, 225, 226, 227, 228, 229ab, 218cd, 232cd, 233, 234,
                    235, 236, 237, 238, 239, 240, 241, 242, 243, 244, 253cd, 254cd, 255,
                    256, 257, , 258, 264, 266ab, 267cd, 268ab, 277, 278, 279, 280ab,
                    281ab, 284cd, 286ab, 295-318, 319cd, 323</p>
                  <p>Additions 124a, 135a, 158a, 160, 201a-201c, 210a-210e, 232a-232b,
                    254a-254c, 273a-273g, 294a-294j, 320a-320b</p>
                  <p>- Chapter begins from verse no 104, folio no. 180r</p>
                  <p>- Verse 134ab is given after 128</p>
                  <p>- There are two folios named 183v. In the first 183v folio, there are
                    7 verses. Content of these 7 verses (273a to 273g) seems
                    different.</p>
                  <p>- Content of 294a to 294j, match with Cakradatta of Cakrapaṇḍita</p>
                </note>

                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.47L <p>Missing verses: 21ab, 22cd,
                    23ab, 29cd, 30ab, 54ab, 75cd, 76, 79ab</p>
                  <p>Additions: 4ef, 11, 12, 54.1ab, 73.1, 73.2, 73.3</p>
                  <p>Metre Break: 31ab, 80ab</p>
                </note>

      <div n="6" type="sthāna">

        <div n="45" type="adhyāya">

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.1">athāto raktapittapratiṣedhaṃ vyā ||</l>



          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3x">vyāyāmabhārādhyayanavyavoyātapaseva<cb n="2"/>naiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tīkṣṇoṣṇakṣāralavaṇaiamlaiḥ kaṭvābhir eva ca |</l>



          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4x">abhikṣṇaṃ sevato tūṣṇo rasaḥ pittaṃ pradūṣayet |
            <caesura/>
             pittaṃ vidagdhaṃ sva<lb n="5"/>guṇaividahaty āśu śoṇitaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.5">tataḥ pravartate raktamūrdhvaṃ cādho dvidhāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             āmāśayād vrajed ūrdhvam adhaḥ <cb n="1"/>pakvāśayād vrajet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6ab">vidagdhayoś cāpy ubhayor dvidhābhāgaṃ pravartate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7ab">ūrdhvaṃ sādhyamadhoyāpyamasādhyaṃ yugapad gataṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6cd"> yakṛn plīhāsyām ichanti kecid rakta<cb n="2"/>gatiṃ
            jānāḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7cd">sadanaṃ śītakāmitvaṃ kaṇṭhadhūmāyanam vamī |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.8">lohagandhiś ca niśvāso bhavaty asmiṃ bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             vāhyāsṛ<lb n="6"/>glakṣaṇais tasya saṃkhyā doṣocchritair viduḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.9">daurvalyaśvāsakāsajvaravathumadā pāṇḍutādāhamūrcchā
            <caesura/>
             bhukte<cb n="1"/> cānne vidāhas tv adhṛtir api sadā hṛdya tulyā ca pīḍā |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇākaṇṭhasya bhedaḥ śirasi ca pavanaṃ pūtiniḥ ṣṭhīvanañ ca
            <caesura/>
             dveṣo bhakte vipāko viratir a<cb n="2"/>pi bhaved raktapittopasargāt ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.10">māṃsaprakṣālanābhaṃ kvathitam api yakṛtkardamāñbhonibham
            vā
            <caesura/>
             medaḥ pūyāstikalpaṃ ya<lb n="7"/>kṛd iva yadi vā pakvajambūphalābham |
            <caesura/>
             yat kṛṣṇaṃ yac ca nīlaṃ bhṛśam atikuṇapaṃ yatra coktā vikārāḥ
            <caesura/>
             tad varjyaṃ ra<cb n="1"/>ktapittaṃ surapatidhanuṣā yac ca tulyaṃ vibhāti
            ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.11">nodṛktam ādau saṃgrāhyaṃ valino bhiṣaja sadā |
            <caesura/>
             hṛt pāṇḍugrahaṇīrogaplīhagulmajvarāvahaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.12"><cb n="2"/>adhaḥ pravṛttaṃ vamanair ūrdhvagan tu
            virecanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jayed anyataraṃ cāpi kṣīṇasya śamanair asṛk |</l>





          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.15">drākṣākārśmayamadhukaṃ <milestone facs="190r IMG_0050"
              n="190r" unit="digital-image"/><pb facs="222" n="190r"/><lb n="1"/>sitāyetaṃ
            virecanaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             yaṣṭhīmadhukasiddhañ ca sakṣaudraṃ vamanaṃ hitaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.16">payāṃsi śītāni rasāś ca jāṅgalāḥ satīnamū<cb n="1"
            />dgāyavaśāliṣaṣṭikā |
            <caesura/>
             jīvanti śailūsuniṣaṇṇayūthikāṃs tathātimuktāṃ kura<damage extent="4"
              unit="char"/>rajāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.17">śākaṃ hitaṃ sarpiṣisaṃskṛtaṃ sadā pathyāñ ca
              dhātrīphaladāḍimā<cb n="2"/>nvitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             rasāś ca pārāvatahaṃsakurmajapeyā peyās tathā cāpi ghṛtāntarā hitāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.18">santānikāś cotpalapūrvakeṣu ghṛteṣu si<lb n="2"/>ddhāḥ
            payasaḥ sitā<unclear>hvā</unclear> |
            <caesura/>
             himāḥ pradehā madhurā gaṇāś ca ghṛtāni pathyāni ca raktapitte |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.19">madhūkaśobhāñja<cb n="1"/>nakodirajaiḥ priyaṃgukānāṃ
            kusumaiś ca cūrṇanitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhiṣag vidadhyāc caturaḥ samākṣikāṃ hitāya lehānasṛjāḥ praśāntaye |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.20">lihyāc ca dugdhadrumajan na<cb n="2"/>vāṃkurāṃ
            madhudvitīyāṃ sitakarṇikasya |
            <caesura/>
             pathyāñ ca kharjūraphalaṃ samākṣikaṃ phalāni cānyānyapitaṇguṇānyatha ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21ab"><lb n="3"/>raktānisārābhihitānyogānatrāpi yojayet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21x">||nilotpalānām madhunā bhasma vāpi parisrutaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21cd"> śuddhekṣugaṇḍamāpoṣya nave kumbhe hitāṃbhasā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.22"> yojayitvā sthitaṃ rātrāvā<cb n="2"/>kāśe sotpalaṃ tu tat
            |
            <caesura/>
             prātaḥ śrutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ pivec choṇitaipittakaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.23">pivec chi<cb n="1"/>takaṣāyaṃ vā jamvāmrārjunasambhavaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             āmodumvaraniryāsaṃ pivet sakṣaudraśarkaraṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.24">trapuśīmūlakalkam vā sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍutālā<lb n="4"/>mvunā
            |
            <caesura/>
             pived akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ madhukalpaivam eva vā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.25">candanaṃ padmaṃ kaṃlodhram evaṃ mevaṃ samaṃ pivet |
            <caesura/>
             karañja<cb n="1"/>vījam evam vā sitākṣaudrayutaṃ pivet |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.26">majjānamidgudasyaivam peyo madhukasaṃyutāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sukhoṣṇalavaṇaṃ vījaṃ karañjadadhimastunā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.27">pived vāpi tryahaṃ<cb n="1"/> martyo raktapittābhipīḍitaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             raktapittaharāḥ śastāḥ ṣaḍete yogam uttamāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.28">pathyā caivāvapīḍeṣu grāṇa<lb n="5"/>taḥ pramṛte sṛji |
            <caesura/>
             atinissrutarakto vā kṣaudrayuktaṃ pivedasṛk |
            <caesura/>
             yakṛd vā bhakṣayed ājāmāṃsaṃ pitta<cb n="1"/>samāyutaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.29">palāśavṛntasvarase vipakvaṃ
            <caesura/>
             sarpi pivet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             saśarkaraṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pived vā
            <caesura/>
             vanaspatīṃ svarasaiḥ kṛtam vā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.30">drākṣāmu<cb n="2"/>śīrāṇy atha padmakaṃ sitā
            <caesura/>
             pṛthak palāṃśyudake samāvayet |
            <caesura/>
             sthitāṃ niśān tad rudhirāmayañ jayet
            <caesura/>
             pītaṃ pa<lb n="6"/>yo vāmvusamaṃ hitāśinā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.31">samākṣikaṃ vājiśakṛdrasaṃ vā
            <caesura/>
             vāsākaṣāyaṃ sahitaṃ pived vā |
            <caesura/>
             lihyāt tathā vā<cb n="1"/>stukavījacūrṇaṃ
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudraplutaṃ taṇḍulasāhvayam vā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.32">liheta kālāñjanacūrṇām eva
            <caesura/>
             liheta vā kṣaudrayutāṃ tu kākhyāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             drāṣāsitātiktakarohiṇīñ ca <cb n="2"/>
            <caesura/>
             himāmvunā vā madhukañ jayeyaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33ab">pathyāmahīṃsrāṃ rajanīṃ ghṭañ ca
            <caesura/>
             lihet tathā śoṇitapittarogī |</l>





          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.36cd">mūlāni <lb n="7"/> puṣpāṇi ca mātuluṅgyāḥ
            <caesura/>
             piṣṭvā pivet taṇḍuladhāvanena |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.37">ghrāṇapravṛtte sṛji nasya muktaṃ
            <caesura/>
             saśarakarāṃ <cb n="2"/>nāsikayoḥ payo vā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣārasaṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pived vā
            <caesura/>
             saśarkaraṃ cekṣurasaṃ hitam vā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.38">śitopacāraṃ madhurañ ca kuryād
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣataḥ śoṇitapitta<cb n="2"/>rogai |
            <caesura/>
             śitāghṛtañ kṣaudrayutena cāpi
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhādigaṇaśritena |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.39">kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanamagryamuktaṃ
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ <damage>gh</damage><milestone facs="190v IMG_0051.jpg" n="190v"
              unit="digital-image"/><pb facs="223" n="190v"/><lb n="1"/>taṃ cāpy
            anuvāsanārthaṃ ||
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭharodhrāñjanagairikotpalaiḥ
            <caesura/>
             suvarṇakālīyakaśaṃkhacandanaiḥ |</l>

            bhavati śokasamudbhave tu |

            |
